[30;1m10 | [0m[35mThis module is a re-implementation aiming for speed instead of maximum[0m
[30;1m11 | [0m[35mcompression, so it can be used at runtime (rather than during a preprocessing[0m
[30;1m12 | [0m[35mstep). RCSSmin does syntactical compression only (removing spaces, comments[0m
[30;1m13 | [0m[35mand possibly semicolons). It does not provide semantic compression (like[0m
[30;1m14 | [0m[35mremoving empty blocks, collapsing redundant properties etc). It does, however,[0m
